 if (newWindow)
 window.open(url, '_blank');
 else

 }

 var loadQueue = [];
 function runOnLoad(fn) { loadQueue.push(fn); }
 window.onload = function() {
 for (var i = 0; i < loadQueue.length; i++)
 loadQueue[i]();
 delete loadQueue;
 };

        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

In [1],  HandleAddStartupPage function doesn't verify if the `args[1]` is a String type variant, and get it as String directly.



<span class="line"><!---->In [1],  HandleAddStartupPage function doesn't verify if the `args[1]` is a String type variant, and get it as String directly.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In [2],  index  from `args[1].GetInt()` doesn't check whether it is less than 0. If the index is less than 0, heap overflow will happened in [3].



<span class="line"><!---->In [2],  index  from `args[1].GetInt()` doesn't check whether it is less than 0. If the index is less than 0, heap overflow will happened in [3].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Note that index could be controlled by sending UI message in JS, when there's a uxss in chromium.



<span class="line"><!---->Note that index could be controlled by sending UI message in JS, when there's a uxss in chromium.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<div class="issue-diff">
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Summary:</strong>
          
          [WebUI] StartupPagesHandler does not adequately verify arguments from JS
          (was: Inappropriate implementation in StartupPagesHandler)
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Status:</strong>
          
          Assigned
          (was: Unconfirmed)
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Owner:</strong>
          
          dpa...@chromium.org
          
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Labels:</strong>
          
          Security_Severity-Medium Security_Impact-Stable
          
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Components:</strong>
          
          UI&gt;Settings

      </div>

<br>


    


        


      


        









Assigning medium severity since:



<span class="line"><!---->Assigning medium severity since:<!----></span>



<br>





1. This is a bug in the validation logic in a browser-side component



<span class="line"><!---->1. This is a bug in the validation logic in a browser-side component<!----></span>



<br>





2. WebUI is normally isolated into its own renderer process and not typically "malicious"



<span class="line"><!---->2. WebUI is normally isolated into its own renderer process and not typically "malicious"<!----></span>



<br>





3. But combined with a UXSS bug that allows arbitrary script execution in a chrome:// renderer would lead to trouble.



<span class="line"><!---->3. But combined with a UXSS bug that allows arbitrary script execution in a chrome:// renderer would lead to trouble.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Any browser-side code that consumes values from the renderer must validate the values. The missing non-negative index check is possibly the worst example, but a fix for this should also audit the other WebUI message callbacks for other memory safety issues / CHECK issues. A malicious renderer should not be able to trigger either issue, even if it's in a WebUI handler.



<span class="line"><!---->Any browser-side code that consumes values from the renderer must validate the values. The missing non-negative index check is possibly the worst example, but a fix for this should also audit the other WebUI message callbacks for other memory safety issues / CHECK issues. A malicious renderer should not be able to trigger either issue, even if it's in a WebUI handler.<!----></span>

<br>





passed from JS, but such a parameter is never actually passed from the

<br>





UI. Moreover the code that was handling it was incrorectly not checking



<span class="line"><!---->UI. Moreover the code that was handling it was incrorectly not checking<!----></span>



<br>





for "greater than zero" opening up the door unnecessarily to potential



<span class="line"><!---->for "greater than zero" opening up the door unnecessarily to potential<!----></span>



<br>





vulnerabilities, if someose manually passes parameters using the



<span class="line"><!---->vulnerabilities, if someose manually passes parameters using the<!----></span>

DevTools console (or if somehow the WebUI page is compromised).



<span class="line"><!---->DevTools console (or if somehow the WebUI page is compromised).<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
